<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vezel.html>vezel</a> (25528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*vesele</i> (from which <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">veselen</i>), from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vese</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-ele</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijzen.html>vees</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-el</i>.  Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fasÅn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">fiber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">faso</i>.
</p>

<ol><li>A fibre <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Commonwealth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; fiber <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">single piece/<a href = vnd.unilang:strand.html>strand</a> of fabric or other material</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>

***viceroy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:viceroy.html>viceroy</a> (34563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">vice-roy</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">vice-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:roy.html>roy</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">king</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:viceroy.html>viceroy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">viceroys</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who governs a country, province, or colony as the representative of a monarch.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">vicar</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">provost</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Ireland <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> governed by a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:viceroy.html>Viceroy</a></b> representing the English King/Queen when it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> part of the United Kingdom of Great Britain and Ireland.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1980</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Lean" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:David Lean">David Lean</a>, <i>A Screenplay of E.M. <a href = vnd.unilang:forster.html>Forster</a>'s A Passage to India</i>, Script City, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=EDnyAAAAMAAJamp;q=%22the+viceroy%27s+on+board%22amp;dq=%22the+viceroy%27s+on+board%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ved=0ahUKEwjg7Zuwj5HbAhXLurwKHSX8AzAQ6AEIMTAC">page 2</a>,
<dl><dd>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:viceroy.html>Viceroy</a>'</b>s on board <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> tends to liven <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> up.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A zongdu.</li>
<li>An orange and black North American butterfly (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Limenitis_archippus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Limenitis archippus"><i>Limenitis archippus</i></a></span>), so named because it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> similar to, but <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> than, the monarch butterfly.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vies.html>vies</a> (2824)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijzen.html>vijs</a></i>, of uncertain origin. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fies</i>.

***vijftig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijftig.html>vijftig</a> (2235)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vijftich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fÄ«ftig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fimf tigiwiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijftig.html>vijftig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>fifty</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although <a href = vnd.unilang:spelt.html>spelt</a> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">v-</i>, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally pronounced with initial <span class="IPA">/f/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in accents that generally do not devoice <i>v-</i>. (This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeventig.html>zeventig</a></i> ["seventy"], which used to have a prefix <i>t-</i> and hence a devoiced <i>z-</i>). However, there are also many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> who pronounce <span class="IPA">/v/</span> in line with the spelling as a hypercorrection.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vijftig.html>vijftig</a></b>
</p>

***vijver.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijver.html>vijver</a> (8777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">viver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">vivier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vÄ«vÄrium</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> merged with or replaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wier.html>wier</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wuwer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*wiwer</i>, an older borrowing directly from Latin; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weiher</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijver.html>vijver</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijvers.html>vijvers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vijvertje.html>vijvertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
